I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
WebAuthn ignores AuthenticationEventPublisher
**Describe the bug**
WebAuthn does not use the configured (global) `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.

looks like `NullEventPublisher` is always used (at least thats what you can see in debug).  
ref. https://github.com/spring-projects/spring-security/blob/7.0.0-RC1/config/src/main/java/org/springframework/security/config/annotation/web/configurers/WebAuthnConfigurer.java#L178-L179

**To Reproduce**
* define an `AuthenticationEventPublisher` bean
* authenticate e.g. with username/password
  * `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` published on the configured `AuthenticationEventPublisher`
* authenticate with a passkey
  * `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` published on a `NullEventPublisher` (and swallowed)

**Expected behavior**
WebAuthn should use the configured (global) `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.

**Sample**

sample app will be referenced asap:
* run
* log in as user / password
  * event listener fired, see log
```
2025-10-28T07:04:30.267+01:00  INFO 32928 --- [demo] [nio-8080-exec-6] com.example.demo.AuthenticationEvents    : AuthenticationEvents onSuccess: org.springframework.security.authentication.event.AuthenticationSuccessEvent[source=UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken [Principal=org.springframework.security.core.userdetails.User [Username=user, Password=[PROTECTED], Enabled=true, AccountNonExpired=true, CredentialsNonExpired=true, AccountNonLocked=true, Granted Authorities=[ROLE_USER]], Credentials=[PROTECTED], Authenticated=true, Details=WebAuthenticationDetails [RemoteIpAddress=127.0.0.1, SessionId=C36A389B691D34D30439DB46090194E2], Granted Authorities=[ROLE_USER, FactorGrantedAuthority [authority=FACTOR_PASSWORD, issuedAt=2025-10-28T06:04:30.265508800Z]]]]
```
* http://localhost:8080/webauthn/register
  * register a passkey
* log out
* log in using passkey
  * event listener not fired

</pr_description>

Can you help me implement the necessary changes to the repository so that the requirements specified in the <pr_description> are met?

   190	                        creationOptionsFilter.setCreationOptionsRepository(creationOptionsRepository);

   194	                        creationOptionsFilter.setConverter(this.converter);
   195	                }
   196	                http.addFilterBefore(webAuthnAuthnFilter, BasicAuthenticationFilter.class);
   197	                http.addFilterAfter(webAuthnRegistrationFilter, AuthorizationFilter.class);

   201	                DefaultLoginPageGeneratingFilter loginPageGeneratingFilter = http

   206	                        loginPageGeneratingFilter.setResolveHeaders((request) -> {
   207	                                CsrfToken csrfToken = (CsrfToken) request.getAttribute(CsrfToken.class.getName());

   231	        }

   233	        private <C> Optional<C> getSharedOrBean(H http, Class<C> type) {
   234	                C shared = http.getSharedObject(type);
   235	                return Optional.ofNullable(shared).or(() -> getBeanOrNull(type));
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        private <T> Optional<T> getBeanOrNull(Class<T> type) {
   239	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   240	                if (context == null) {
   241	                        return Optional.empty();
   242	                }
   243	                try {
   244	                        return Optional.of(context.getBean(type));
   245	                }
   246	                catch (NoSuchBeanDefinitionException ex) {
   247	                        return Optional.empty();
   248	                }
   249	        }

   116	                }
   117	                if (event != null) {
   118	                        if (this.applicationEventPublisher != null) {
   119	                                this.applicationEventPublisher.publishEvent(event);
   120	                        }
   121	                }
   122	                else {
   123	                        if (this.logger.isDebugEnabled()) {
   124	                                this.logger.debug("No event was found for the exception " + exception.getClass().getName());
   125	                        }
   126	                }
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        private @Nullable Constructor<? extends AbstractAuthenticationEvent> getEventConstructor(
   130	                        AuthenticationException exception) {
   131	                Constructor<? extends AbstractAuthenticationEvent> eventConstructor = this.exceptionMappings
   132	                        .get(exception.getClass().getName());
   133	                return (eventConstructor != null) ? eventConstructor : this.defaultAuthenticationFailureEventConstructor;
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        @Override
   137	        public void setApplicationEventPublisher(ApplicationEventPublisher applicationEventPublisher) {
   138	                this.applicationEventPublisher = applicationEventPublisher;
   139	        }
   140

    27	import org.springframework.security.web.DefaultSecurityFilterChain;
    28	import org.springframework.security.web.servlet.util.matcher.PathPatternRequestMatcher;
    29	
    30	/**
    31	 * Adds a convenient base class for {@link SecurityConfigurer} instances that operate on
    32	 * {@link HttpSecurity}.
    33	 *
    34	 * @author Rob Winch
    35	 * @author Ding Hao
    36	 */
    37	public abstract class AbstractHttpConfigurer<T extends AbstractHttpConfigurer<T, B>, B extends HttpSecurityBuilder<B>>
    38	                extends SecurityConfigurerAdapter<DefaultSecurityFilterChain, B> {
    39	
    40	        private SecurityContextHolderStrategy securityContextHolderStrategy;
    41	
    42	        /**
    43	         * Disables the {@link AbstractHttpConfigurer} by removing it. After doing so a fresh
    44	         * version of the configuration can be applied.
    45	         * @return the {@link HttpSecurityBuilder} for additional customizations
    46	         */
    47	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    48	        public B disable() {
    49	                getBuilder().removeConfigurer(getClass());
    50	                return getBuilder();
    51	        }
    52	
    53	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    54	        public T withObjectPostProcessor(ObjectPostProcessor<?> objectPostProcessor) {
    55	                addObjectPostProcessor(objectPostProcessor);
    56	                return (T) this;
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        protected SecurityContextHolderStrategy getSecurityContextHolderStrategy() {
    60	                if (this.securityContextHolderStrategy != null) {
    61	                        return this.securityContextHolderStrategy;
    62	                }
    63	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
    64	                this.securityContextHolderStrategy = context.getBeanProvider(SecurityContextHolderStrategy.class)
    65	                        .getIfUnique(SecurityContextHolder::getContextHolderStrategy);
    66	                return this.securityContextHolderStrategy;
    67	        }
    68	
    69	        protected PathPatternRequestMatcher.Builder getRequestMatcherBuilder() {
    70	                return getBuilder().getSharedObject(PathPatternRequestMatcher.Builder.class);
    71	        }
    72	
    73	}

    17	package org.springframework.security.config.annotation;
    18	
    19	import java.util.ArrayList;
    20	import java.util.List;
    21	
    22	import org.springframework.core.GenericTypeResolver;
    23	import org.springframework.core.annotation.AnnotationAwareOrderComparator;
    24	import org.springframework.security.config.Customizer;
    25	import org.springframework.security.config.ObjectPostProcessor;
    26	import org.springframework.util.Assert;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * A base class for {@link SecurityConfigurer} that allows subclasses to only implement
    30	 * the methods they are interested in. It also provides a mechanism for using the
    31	 * {@link SecurityConfigurer} and when done gaining access to the {@link SecurityBuilder}
    32	 * that is being configured.
    33	 *
    34	 * @param <O> The Object being built by B
    35	 * @param <B> The Builder that is building O and is configured by
    36	 * {@link SecurityConfigurerAdapter}
    37	 * @author Rob Winch
    38	 * @author Wallace Wadge
    39	 */
    40	public abstract class SecurityConfigurerAdapter<O, B extends SecurityBuilder<O>> implements SecurityConfigurer<O, B> {
    41	
    42	        private B securityBuilder;
    43	
    44	        private CompositeObjectPostProcessor objectPostProcessor = new CompositeObjectPostProcessor();
    45	
    46	        @Override
    47	        public void init(B builder) {
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        @Override
    51	        public void configure(B builder) {
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        /**
    55	         * Gets the {@link SecurityBuilder}. Cannot be null.
    56	         * @return the {@link SecurityBuilder}
    57	         * @throws IllegalStateException if {@link SecurityBuilder} is null
    58	         */
    59	        protected final B getBuilder() {
    60	                Assert.state(this.securityBuilder != null, "securityBuilder cannot be null");
    61	                return this.securityBuilder;
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        /**
    65	         * Performs post processing of an object. The default is to delegate to the
    66	         * {@link ObjectPostProcessor}.
    67	         * @param object the Object to post process
    68	         * @return the possibly modified Object to use
    69	         */
    70	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    71	        protected <T> T postProcess(T object) {
    72	                return (T) this.objectPostProcessor.postProcess(object);
    73	        }
    74	
    75	        /**
    76	         * Adds an {@link ObjectPostProcessor} to be used for this
    77	         * {@link SecurityConfigurerAdapter}. The default implementation does nothing to the
    78	         * object.
    79	         * @param objectPostProcessor the {@link ObjectPostProcessor} to use
    80	         */
    81	        public void addObjectPostProcessor(ObjectPostProcessor<?> objectPostProcessor) {
    82	                this.objectPostProcessor.addObjectPostProcessor(objectPostProcessor);
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        /**
    86	         * Sets the {@link SecurityBuilder} to be used. This is automatically set when using
    87	         * {@link AbstractConfiguredSecurityBuilder#with(SecurityConfigurerAdapter, Customizer)}
    88	         * @param builder the {@link SecurityBuilder} to set
    89	         */
    90	        public void setBuilder(B builder) {
    91	                this.securityBuilder = builder;
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        /**
    95	         * An {@link ObjectPostProcessor} that delegates work to numerous
    96	         * {@link ObjectPostProcessor} implementations.
    97	         *
    98	         * @author Rob Winch
    99	         */
   100	        private static final class CompositeObjectPostProcessor implements ObjectPostProcessor<Object> {
   101	
   102	                private List<ObjectPostProcessor<?>> postProcessors = new ArrayList<>();
   103	
   104	                @Override
   105	                @SuppressWarnings({ "rawtypes", "unchecked" })
   106	                public Object postProcess(Object object) {
   107	                        for (ObjectPostProcessor opp : this.postProcessors) {
   108	                                Class<?> oppClass = opp.getClass();
   109	                                Class<?> oppType = GenericTypeResolver.resolveTypeArgument(oppClass, ObjectPostProcessor.class);
   110	                                if (oppType == null || oppType.isAssignableFrom(object.getClass())) {
   111	                                        object = opp.postProcess(object);
   112	                                }
   113	                        }
   114	                        return object;
   115	                }
   116	
   117	                /**
   118	                 * Adds an {@link ObjectPostProcessor} to use
   119	                 * @param objectPostProcessor the {@link ObjectPostProcessor} to add
   120	                 * @return true if the {@link ObjectPostProcessor} was added, else false
   121	                 */
   122	                private boolean addObjectPostProcessor(ObjectPostProcessor<?> objectPostProcessor) {
   123	                        boolean result = this.postProcessors.add(objectPostProcessor);
   124	                        this.postProcessors.sort(AnnotationAwareOrderComparator.INSTANCE);
   125	                        return result;
   126	                }
   127	
   128	        }
   129	
   130	}

    28	import org.springframework.beans.factory.InitializingBean;
    29	import org.springframework.beans.factory.ObjectProvider;
    30	import org.springframework.beans.factory.SmartInitializingSingleton;
    31	import org.springframework.beans.factory.config.AutowireCapableBeanFactory;
    32	import org.springframework.core.NativeDetector;
    33	import org.springframework.security.config.ObjectPostProcessor;
    34	import org.springframework.util.Assert;
    35	
    36	/**
    37	 * Allows registering Objects to participate with an {@link AutowireCapableBeanFactory}'s
    38	 * post processing of {@link Aware} methods, {@link InitializingBean#afterPropertiesSet()}
    39	 * , and {@link DisposableBean#destroy()}.
    40	 *
    41	 * @author Rob Winch
    42	 * @since 3.2
    43	 */
    44	final class AutowireBeanFactoryObjectPostProcessor
    45	                implements ObjectPostProcessor<Object>, DisposableBean, SmartInitializingSingleton {
    46	
    47	        private final Log logger = LogFactory.getLog(getClass());
    48	
    49	        private final AutowireCapableBeanFactory autowireBeanFactory;
    50	
    51	        private final List<DisposableBean> disposableBeans = new ArrayList<>();
    52	
    53	        private final List<SmartInitializingSingleton> smartSingletons = new ArrayList<>();
    54	
    55	        AutowireBeanFactoryObjectPostProcessor(AutowireCapableBeanFactory autowireBeanFactory) {
    56	                Assert.notNull(autowireBeanFactory, "autowireBeanFactory cannot be null");
    57	                this.autowireBeanFactory = autowireBeanFactory;
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        @Override
    61	        public <T> T postProcess(T object) {
    62	                if (object == null) {
    63	                        return null;
    64	                }
    65	                T result = null;
    66	                try {
    67	                        result = initializeBeanIfNeeded(object);
    68	                }
    69	                catch (RuntimeException ex) {
    70	                        Class<?> type = object.getClass();
    71	                        throw new RuntimeException("Could not postProcess " + object + " of type " + type, ex);
    72	                }
    73	                this.autowireBeanFactory.autowireBean(object);
    74	                if (result instanceof DisposableBean) {
    75	                        this.disposableBeans.add((DisposableBean) result);
    76	                }
    77	                if (result instanceof SmartInitializingSingleton) {
    78	                        this.smartSingletons.add((SmartInitializingSingleton) result);
    79	                }
    80	                return result;
    81	        }
    82	
    83	        /**
    84	         * Invokes {@link AutowireCapableBeanFactory#initializeBean(Object, String)} only if
    85	         * needed, i.e when the application is not a native image or the object is not a CGLIB
    86	         * proxy.
    87	         * @param object the object to initialize
    88	         * @param <T> the type of the object
    89	         * @return the initialized bean or an existing bean if the object is a CGLIB proxy and
    90	         * the application is a native image
    91	         * @see <a href=
    92	         * "https://github.com/spring-projects/spring-security/issues/14825">Issue
    93	         * gh-14825</a>
    94	         */
    95	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    96	        private <T> T initializeBeanIfNeeded(T object) {
    97	                if (!NativeDetector.inNativeImage() || !AopUtils.isCglibProxy(object)) {
    98	                        return (T) this.autowireBeanFactory.initializeBean(object, object.toString());
    99	                }
   100	                ObjectProvider<?> provider = this.autowireBeanFactory.getBeanProvider(object.getClass());
   101	                Object bean = provider.getIfUnique();
   102	                if (bean == null) {
   103	                        String msg = """
   104	                                        Failed to resolve an unique bean (single or primary) of type [%s] from the BeanFactory.
   105	                                        Because the object is a CGLIB Proxy, a raw bean cannot be initialized during runtime in a native image.
   106	                                        """
   107	                                .formatted(object.getClass());
   108	                        throw new IllegalStateException(msg);
   109	                }
   110	                return (T) bean;
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        @Override
   114	        public void afterSingletonsInstantiated() {
   115	                for (SmartInitializingSingleton singleton : this.smartSingletons) {
   116	                        singleton.afterSingletonsInstantiated();
   117	                }
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        @Override

🎬 ACTION
cat > /tmp/reproduce-webauthn-event-publisher.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
file=/testbed/config/src/main/java/org/springframework/security/config/annotation/web/configurers/WebAuthnConfigurer.java
if grep -q "setAuthenticationEventPublisher" "$file"; then
  echo "FIXED: WebAuthnConfigurer wires an AuthenticationEventPublisher into its ProviderManager"
  exit 0
fi
echo "BUG: WebAuthnConfigurer creates a ProviderManager for WebAuthn without setAuthenticationEventPublisher, so ProviderManager uses NullEventPublisher"
awk 'NR>=176 && NR<=181 { print NR ":" $0 }' "$file"
exit 1
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/reproduce-webauthn-event-publisher.sh

-/**
- * We need to compile with JDK 25 for nullability support, but using JDK 25 means that our tests will fail due to the
- * <a href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/25/security/security-manager-is-permanently-disabled.html">removal
- * of the Java Security Manager</a>. For example, in JDK 25 {@code Subject.getSubject(AccessControlContext)} throws an
- * {@code UnsupportedOperationException}.
- *
- * To resolve this, we must migrate tests to use the new APIs (e.g. {@code Subject.current()}) but those APIs are not
- * available in the JDK 17 source, so compiling with JDK 25 and release 17 fails. The plugin overrides the test
- * compilation to use release 25.
- *
- * @see <a href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/25/security/security-manager-is-permanently-disabled.html">The
- * Security Manager Is Permanently Disabled</a>
- * @see <a href="https://inside.java/2024/07/08/quality-heads-up/">Quality Outreach Heads-up - JDK 23: Re-Specified
- * Subject.getSubject API</a>
- */
-

-	if (task.name == 'compileTestJava' || task.name == 'compileIntegrationTestJava') {

cat > buildSrc/src/main/groovy/test-compile-target-jdk25.gradle <<'EOF'
import org.gradle.api.tasks.compile.JavaCompile
import org.jetbrains.kotlin.gradle.tasks.KotlinCompile

/**
 * We need to compile with JDK 25 for nullability support, but using JDK 25 means that our tests will fail due to the
 * <a href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/25/security/security-manager-is-permanently-disabled.html">removal
 * of the Java Security Manager</a>. For example, in JDK 25 {@code Subject.getSubject(AccessControlContext)} throws an
 * {@code UnsupportedOperationException}.
 *
 * To resolve this, we must migrate tests to use the new APIs (e.g. {@code Subject.current()}) but those APIs are not
 * available in the JDK 17 source, so compiling with JDK 25 and release 17 fails. The plugin overrides the test
 * compilation to use release 25.
 *
 * @see <a href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/25/security/security-manager-is-permanently-disabled.html">The
 * Security Manager Is Permanently Disabled</a>
 * @see <a href="https://inside.java/2024/07/08/quality-heads-up/">Quality Outreach Heads-up - JDK 23: Re-Specified
 * Subject.getSubject API</a>
 */

tasks.withType(JavaCompile).configureEach { task ->

	}
}
